	#Subjugate The Trade Tribe
	focus = {
		id = Generic_subjugate_the_trade_tribe
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_demand_territory
		x = 0
		y = 3
		cost = 10
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION
		}
		available= {
    any_neighbor_country = {
            not = {
                is_guaranteed_by = ROOT # not guaranteed by us
                is_in_faction_with = ROOT # not in faction with us
                has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT #  # no non aggression by us
                is_subject_of = ROOT # not our puppet or subject
				tag = XXX
            }
        }
    }

		prerequisite = { focus = Generic_influence_through_overwhelming_force  } prerequisite = { focus = Generic_rally_our_ranks  }
		completion_reward = {
			# first we scope to a random nation
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { # some sanity checks
					not = {
						is_guaranteed_by = ROOT # not guaranteed by us
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT # not in faction with us
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT #  # no non aggression by us
						is_subject_of = ROOT # not our puppet or subject
						tag = XXX
					}
				}
				ROOT = { # we scope back to our own country
					create_wargoal = { # declare war on
						target = PREV # previous scope (random neighbor)
						type = annex_everything # standard wargoal
					}
				}
    }
}
	}

	#Implement A Currency
	focus = {
		id = Generic_implement_a_currency
		icon = GFX_focus_fra_devalue_the_franc
		x = 4
		y = 6
		cost = 5
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY
		}
		completion_reward = {
		
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_1_base } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_1_base 
					add_idea = society_2_base_currency
				}
				}

				else = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = society_1_base
						add_idea = society_2_base_currency
					}
				}
				
				add_political_power = 50


		}
	}

	#Protect Commercial Trade
	focus = {
		id = Generic_protect_commercial_trade
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_positive_trade_relations
		x = 3
		y = 7
		cost = 5
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = Generic_implement_a_currency  }
		completion_reward = {
		
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_2_base_currency } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_2_base_currency 
					add_idea = society_3_base_currency_commercial
				}
			}

			else = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = society_2_base_currency
						add_idea = society_3_base_currency_commercial
					}
				}
				
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = industrial_complex
										size > 1
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}




		}
	}

	#Protect Private Property
	focus = {
		id = Generic_protect_private_property
		icon = GFX_PAZ_protect_private_property-646314
		x = 5
		y = 8
		cost = 5
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY
		}
		prerequisite = { focus = Generic_create_permanent_settlements } prerequisite = { focus = Generic_protect_commercial_trade }
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_3_base_currency_commercial } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_3_base_currency_commercial 
					add_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_property
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_trade } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_trade 
					add_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_property_trade
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_workforce } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_workforce 
					add_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_property_workforce

			else_if = {

					remove_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_trade_workforce

				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_4_base_currency_commercial_border }

					add_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_property_trade_border
				}

			else_if = {

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_workforce_border 
					add_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_property_workforce_border
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_trade_workforce_border } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_trade_workforce_border 
					add_idea = society_7_base_currency_commercial_property_trade_workforce_border
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_trade_border_autonomy } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_trade_border_autonomy 
					add_idea = society_7_base_currency_commercial_property_trade_border_autonomy
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_7_base_currency_commercial_trade_workforce_border_autonomy } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_7_base_currency_commercial_trade_workforce_border_autonomy 
					add_idea = society_8_base_currency_commercial_property_trade_workforce_border_autonomy
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_workforce_labour } 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = society_5_base_currency_commercial_workforce_labour 
					add_idea = society_6_base_currency_commercial_property_workforce_labour
				}

					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = industrial_complex
										size > 1
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
